 </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Chevron (\n         <a href="/wiki/Port_Fourchon,_Louisiana" title="Port Fourchon, Louisiana">\n          Port Fourchon\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         53,000\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         200,000\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Venice Energy Services (\n         <a href="/wiki/Venice,_Louisiana" title="Venice, Louisiana">\n          Venice\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         25,000\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         95,000\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Shell Pipeline Oil (Nairn)\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         13,440\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         50,900\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Sundown Energy (West Potash)\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         13,000\n        </td>\n        <td style="text-align:right;">\n         49,000\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Katrina also had a profound impact on the environment. The storm surge caused substantial\n       <a href="/wiki/Coastal_erosion" title="Coastal erosion">\n        beach erosion\n       </a>\n       , in some cases completely devastating coastal areas. In Dauphin Island (a\n       <a href="/wiki/Barrier_island" title="Barrier island">\n        barrier island\n       </a>\n       ), approximately 90\xc2\xa0mi (140\xc2\xa0km) to the east of the point where the hurricane made landfall, the sand that comprised the island was transported across the island into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_Sound" title="Mississippi Sound">\n        Mississippi Sound\n       </a>\n       , pushing the island towards land.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm surge and waves from Katrina also severely damaged the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chandeleur_Islands" title="Chandeleur Islands">\n        Chandeleur Islands\n       </a>\n       , which had been affected by Hurricane Ivan the previous year.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">\n        <a href="#cite_note-103">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The US Geological Survey has estimated 217\xc2\xa0sq\xc2\xa0mi (560\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ) of land was transformed to water by the hurricanes Katrina and Rita.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Before the storm,\n       <a href="/wiki/Subsidence" title="Subsidence">\n        subsidence\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Erosion" title="Erosion">\n        erosion\n       </a>\n       caused loss of land in the Louisiana wetlands and\n       <a href="/wiki/Bayou" title="Bayou">\n        bayous\n       </a>\n       . This, along with the canals built in the area, let Katrina keep more of its intensity when it struck.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The lands that were lost were breeding grounds for marine mammals, brown\n       <a href="/wiki/Pelican" title="Pelican">\n        pelicans\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Turtle" title="Turtle">\n        turtles\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Fish" title="Fish">\n        fish\n       </a>\n       , and migratory species such as\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Redhead_duck" title="Redhead duck">\n        redhead ducks\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CRS_environment_93-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CRS_environment-93">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Overall, about 20% of the local\n       <a href="/wiki/Marsh" title="Marsh">\n        marshes\n       </a>\n       were permanently overrun by water as a result of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CRS_environment_93-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CRS_environment-93">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The damage from Katrina forced the closure of 16\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Wildlife_Refuge" title="National Wildlife Refuge">\n        National Wildlife Refuges\n       </a>\n       . Breton National Wildlife Refuge lost half its area in the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FWS_impact_106-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FWS_impact-106">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As a result, the hurricane affected the habitats of\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_turtle" title="Sea turtle">\n        sea turtles\n       </a>\n       , Mississippi\n       <a href="/wiki/Sandhill_crane" title="Sandhill crane">\n        sandhill cranes\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Red-cockaded_woodpecker" title="Red-cockaded woodpecker">\n        Red-cockaded woodpeckers\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alabama_Beach_Mouse" title="Alabama Beach Mouse">\n        Alabama Beach mice\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FWS_impact_106-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FWS_impact-106">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Katrina also produced massive tree loss along the Gulf Coast, particularly in Louisiana\'a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pearl_River_Basin" title="Pearl River Basin">\n        Pearl River Basin\n       </a>\n       and among\n       <a href="/wiki/Bottomland_hardwood_forest" title="Bottomland hardwood forest">\n        bottomland hardwood forests\n       </a>\n       . Before the storm the standard mortality rate for the area\'s trees was 1.9%, but this interval increased to 20.5% by the end of 2006.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n        <a href="#cite_note-107">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Delayed mortality as an effect of the storm continued with rates up to 5% until 2011.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This significant loss in\n       <a href="/wiki/Biomass" title="Biomass">\n        biomass\n       </a>\n       caused greater decay and an increase in carbon emissions. For example, by 2006 the decreased biomass in bottomland hardwood forests contributed an amount of carbon which equated to roughly 140% of the net annual U.S.\n       <a href="/wiki/Carbon_sink" title="Carbon sink">\n        carbon sink\n       </a>\n       in forest trees.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">\n        <a href="#cite_note-109">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Chandeleur_L5_Oct2004Sep2005.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="356" data-file-width="540" height="145" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Chandeleur_L5_Oct2004Sep2005.jpg/220px-Chandeleur_L5_Oct2004Sep2005.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Chandeleur_L5_Oct2004Sep2005.jpg/330px-Chandeleur_L5_Oct2004Sep2005.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Chandeleur_L5_Oct2004Sep2005.jpg/440px-Chandeleur_L5_Oct2004Sep2005.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Chandeleur_L5_Oct2004Sep2005.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The\n         <a href="/wiki/Chandeleur_Islands" title="Chandeleur Islands">\n          Chandeleur Islands\n         </a>\n         , before Katrina (left) and after (right), showing the impact of the storm along coastal areas.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The storm caused\n       <a href="/wiki/Oil_spill" title="Oil spill">\n        oil spills\n       </a>\n       from 44 facilities throughout southeastern Louisiana, which resulted in over 7\xc2\xa0million US gallons (26,000\xc2\xa0m\n       <sup>\n        3\n       </sup>\n       ) of\n       <a href="/wiki/Oil" title="Oil">\n        oil\n       </a>\n       being leaked. Some spills were only a few hundred gallons and most were contained on-site, though some oil entered the ecosystem and residential areas. After a spill at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Murphy_Oil" title="Murphy Oil">\n        Murphy Oil\n       </a>\n       refinery, for example, 1,800\xc2\xa0homes were oiled in the towns of\n       <a href="/wiki/Chalmette,_Louisiana" title="Chalmette, Louisiana">\n        Chalmette\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Meraux,_Louisiana" title="Meraux, Louisiana">\n        Meraux\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-msnbcspills_101-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-msnbcspills-101">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Unlike\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ivan" title="Hurricane Ivan">\n        Hurricane Ivan\n       </a>\n       no offshore oil spills were officially reported after Hurricane Katrina. However, Skytruth reported some signs of surface oil in the Gulf of Mexico.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-msnbcspills_101-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-msnbcspills-101">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Finally, as part of the cleanup effort, the flood waters that covered New Orleans were pumped into Lake Pontchartrain, a process that took 43 days to complete.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-katreport_48-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-katreport-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These residual waters contained a mix of raw\n       <a href="/wiki/Sewage" title="Sewage">\n        sewage\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bacteria" title="Bacteria">\n        bacteria\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Heavy_metals" title="Heavy metals">\n        heavy metals\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Pesticide" title="Pesticide">\n        pesticides\n       </a>\n       , toxic chemicals, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Oil" title="Oil">\n        oil\n       </a>\n       , which sparked fears in the scientific community of massive numbers of fish dying.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CRS_environment_93-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CRS_environment-93">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Reestablishing_governance">\n        Reestablishing governance\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Further information:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Katrina_in_New_Orleans#Civil_disturbances" title="Effects of Hurricane Katrina in New Orleans">\n        Effects of Hurricane Katrina in New Orleans \xc2\xa7\xc2\xa0Civil disturbances\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Patrolling_an_area_that_was_previously_underwater_in_New_Orleans_September_2005.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1810" data-file-width="1222" Orleans in an area previously underwater, September 2005.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:USBP-SRT-New_Orleans.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3328" data-file-width="4992" height="147" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/USBP-SRT-New_Orleans.jpg/330px-USBP-SRT-New_Orleans.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/14/USBP-SRT-New_Orleans.jpg/440px-USBP-SRT-New_Orleans.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:USBP-SRT-New_Orleans.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A\n         <a href="/wiki/United_States_Border_Patrol" title="United States Border Patrol">\n          Border Patrol\n         </a>\n         Special Response Team searches a hotel room-by-room in New Orleans in response to Hurricane Katrina.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:La_Nouvelle-Orl%C3%A9ans.jpg">\n         <img alt="La Nouvelle-Orl\xc3\xa9ans.jpg" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/La_Nouvelle-Orl%C3%A9ans.jpg/220px-La_Nouvelle-Orl%C3%A9ans.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/La_Nouvelle-Orl%C3%A9ans.jpg/330px-La_Nouvelle-Orl%C3%A9ans.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a3/La_Nouvelle-Orl%C3%A9ans.jpg/440px-La_Nouvelle-Orl%C3%A9ans.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:La_Nouvelle-Orl%C3%A9ans.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Shortly after the hurricane moved away on August 30, 2005, some residents of New Orleans who remained in the city began\n       <a href="/wiki/Looting" title="Looting">\n        looting\n       </a>\n       stores. Many were in search of food and water that were not available to them through any other means, as well as non-essential items.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">\n        <a href="#cite_note-110">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additionally, there were reports of\n       <a href="/wiki/Carjacking" title="Carjacking">\n        carjacking\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Murder" title="Murder">\n        murders\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Theft" title="Theft">\n        thefts\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Rape" title="Rape">\n        rapes\n       </a>\n       in New Orleans. Some sources later determined that many of the reports were inaccurate, greatly exaggerated or completely false, leading news agencies to print retractions.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">\n        <a href="#cite_note-111">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Thousands of National Guard and federal troops were mobilized and sent to Louisiana, with 7,841 in the area on August 29, to a maximum of 46,838 on September 10. A number of local law enforcement agents from across the country were temporarily deputized by the state. "They have\n       <a href="/wiki/M16_rifle" title="M16 rifle">\n        M16s\n       </a>\n       and are locked and loaded. These troops know how to shoot and kill and I expect they will," Louisiana Governor Kathleen Blanco said.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112">\n        <a href="#cite_note-112">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Congressman\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bill_Jefferson" title="Bill Jefferson">\n        Bill Jefferson\n       </a>\n       told\n       <a href="/wiki/ABC_News" title="ABC News">\n        ABC News\n       </a>\n       : "There was shooting going on. There was sniping going on. Over the first week of September, law and order were gradually restored to the city."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n        <a href="#cite_note-113">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Several shootings occurred between police and New Orleans residents, some involving\n       <a href="/wiki/Police_misconduct" title="Police misconduct">\n        police misconduct\n       </a>\n       ; including\n       <a href="/wiki/Danziger_Bridge_shootings" title="Danziger Bridge shootings">\n        an incident\n       </a>\n       that killed two unarmed civilians and seriously injured other others at\n       <a href="/wiki/Danziger_Bridge" title="Danziger Bridge">\n        Danziger Bridge\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">\n        <a href="#cite_note-114">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Five former police officers pleaded guilty to charges connected to the Danziger Bridge shootings in the aftermath of the hurricane. Six other former or current officers appeared in court in June 2011.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Overall, a number of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arrests" title="Arrests">\n        arrests\n       </a>\n       were made throughout the affected area, including some near the New Orleans Convention Center. A temporary jail was constructed of chain link cages in the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans_Union_Passenger_Terminal" title="New Orleans Union Passenger Terminal">\n        New Orleans Union Passenger Terminal\n       </a>\n       , the city\'s main train station.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In West Virginia, where roughly 350 refugees were located, local officials took fingerprints to run criminal background checks on the refugees. The background checks found that 45% of the refugees had a criminal record of some nature, and that 22% had a violent criminal record.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WBOY_WV_records_117-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WBOY_WV_records-117">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Media speculation fueled a popular perception that the displaced New Orleans residents brought a wave of crime into the communities where they relocated, however, detailed studies of crime statistics in these communities did not reveal a significant increase in violent crime.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">\n        <a href="#cite_note-118">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">\n        <a href="#cite_note-119">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-120">\n        <a href="#cite_note-120">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Government_response">\n        Government response\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Katrina_x_large.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Katrina_x_large.png/450px-Katrina_x_large.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Katrina_x_large.png/600px-Katrina_x_large.png 2x" width="300"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Katrina_x_large.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Chart showing some common uses of the FEMA marking system in\n         <a href="/wiki/New_Orleans" title="New Orleans">\n          New Orleans\n         </a>\n         after Hurricane Katrina\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:BUSHKATRINA.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="343" data-file-width="515"
